[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue: AddressSanitizer reports an attempting double-free on a pointer at [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x5020000000b0[0m[39m in thread T0.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type: memory corruption [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdouble-free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Crash signature:  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • First free at api.[0m[1;92mc:3580[0m[39m inside LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Second free at the same location, indicating the same pointer is freed twice.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Original allocation via malloc [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlFuzzMalloc[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m → xmlStrndup → xmlNewComment.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant observations and findings:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The offending pointer is allocated through the fuzzing allocator [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlFuzzMalloc[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min fuzz/fuzz.c at xmlFuzzMalloc → xmlStrndup → xmlNewComment [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree.[0m[1;92mc:2583[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput [0m[1;39m([0m[39mapi.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m performs a free on that pointer, then under [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer harness maintains a fixed array `vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` of allocated [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlChar* buffers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia xmlFuzzMalloc/xmlStrdup[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and, separately, an array [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vars->nodes[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` of xmlNodePtr trees.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On operations like OP_XML_NEW_COMMENT, the harness does:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        xmlNodePtr cur = [0m[1;35mxmlNewComment[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mgetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mregIdx[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     where `[0m[1;35mgetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[39mregIdx[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returns a pointer into `vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mregIdx[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Internally `xmlNewComment` calls `[0m[1;35mxmlStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, allocating a *new* [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer for `cur->content`.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - At the end of each test, the harness:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Frees **all** entries in `vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlFree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Frees **all** `vars->nodes[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` via `[0m[1;35mdropNode[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → `[0m[1;35mxmlFreeNode[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` → which [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrees `cur->content`.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Under certain sequences, the same pointer can end up in both `vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `cur->content` [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., via other get/set string ops[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so the final-loop free of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` ends up double-freeing that same heap block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfirst in the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrings-cleanup loop, then in dropNode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Eliminate Double-Free[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Ownership Transfer in OP_XML_NEW_COMMENT[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In the harness code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/api.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, locate the handler for the “new comment” [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mopcode [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m1339[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Immediately after calling `[0m[1;35mxmlNewComment[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mgetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[39msrcReg[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, explicitly [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msrcReg[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and then zero out [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that register slot:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msrcReg[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msrcReg[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = NULL;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        This:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Ensures the original buffer passed into `xmlNewComment` is freed exactly[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monce [0m[1;39m([0m[39mright away[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Prevents the final cleanup loop from freeing it again.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Leaves `cur->content` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe duplicate inside the node[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to be freed once [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby `xmlFreeNode` in `dropNode`.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Generalize to All “Consume-String” Ops[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Review other harness opcodes that “consume” a string buffer as part of [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreating or transforming a node [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., processing PI nodes, CDATA sections, or any [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAPI that takes ownership of a user-supplied xmlChar*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - For each such opcode:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          • Immediately free & NULL the source string register after passing it [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto the libxml2 API.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          • This pattern cleanly transfers ownership of that memory into the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibxml2 data structures.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Preserve Existing Harness Cleanup[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Keep the final two loops [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfreeing `vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and then dropping [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vars->nodes[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m intact.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - By NULL’ing consumed string registers, we guarantee the final [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring-cleanup loop skips freed slots and no double-frees occur.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `fuzz/api.c`.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Identify the switch-case [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor if-else[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m block for the OP_XML_NEW_COMMENT [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandler at ~line [0m[1;36m1339[0m[39m.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. After the `[0m[1;35mxmlNewComment[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call but before storing the new node in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vars->nodes[0m[1;39m[[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, insert:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msrcReg[0m[1;39m][0m[39m != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msrcReg[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msrcReg[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = NULL;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Repeat step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m for any other opcode in the harness that hands off a [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mX[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` buffer directly to a libxml2 API that takes over ownership.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Rebuild and rerun the fuzzer harness under AddressSanitizer to confirm the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free no longer occurs and no memory leaks are significant.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach preserves the existing cleanup logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtwo-phase cleanup of [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrings then nodes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, retains all API semantics, and introduces minimal harness code[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By freeing the source buffer immediately upon transfer to libxml2, we [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminate any window where the same pointer is listed twice in the final cleanup.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external libraries, tests, or harness entry-point logic are modified, only [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe minimal ownership bookkeeping in the fuzzer’s API harness.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Immediate free of the source string register may introduce transient memory [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeallocations earlier in the run, but the fuzzer harness is designed for aggressive[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation/deallocation, and libxml2’s own usage remains unaffected.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No existing tests or harness inputs change behavior, since all deallocations [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhappen at program-end or node-teardown, and we only shift the timing of freeing the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muser buffer.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After patching, reproduce the original minimal testcase under ASan with [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`-[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m`.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm no double-free reports occur.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Optionally run the full libFuzzer suite to ensure no new memory-safety issues [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mare introduced.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Locate the cleanup section in fuzz/api.c around line [0m[1;36m3580[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39minside [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLLVMFuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where it currently does something akin to:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < STR_REG_COUNT; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Immediately followed by node cleanup:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < NODE_REG_COUNT; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mdropNode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->nodes[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace the “blind free” of each string register with a “once-only free” [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithm:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Iterate over each string register index `i`.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Let `p = vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`; if `p == NULL`, continue.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Check all earlier registers `k < i`; if any `vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mk[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == p`, skip [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreeing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthis pointer was already freed[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. If not seen before, call `[0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. In either case, clear `vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = NULL` to avoid dangling pointers.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This ensures each unique allocation is freed exactly once, and duplicate [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregister entries do not trigger a second free.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Keep the node cleanup [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dropNode`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m loop unchanged; it frees xmlNode trees and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheir internal memory but will now never interact with freed string-register [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointers.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Example pseudocode patch in fuzz/api.c:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       int i, j;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < STR_REG_COUNT; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           xmlChar *p = vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mp == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             continue;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[35m/[0m[39m* only free the first occurrence of p *[0m[35m/[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; j < i; j++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == p[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               break;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj == i[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = NULL;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[39m* then: for each node register: [0m[1;35mdropNode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->nodes[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; *[0m[35m/[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The AddressSanitizer backtrace shows the same pointer in two registers being [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed twice during cleanup.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This strategy prevents double-free by tracking which pointers have already [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeen freed in the string-register array.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It has minimal impact on existing logic: we still free every unique string [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation exactly once; we do not alter op-handling or fuzz harness.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Node cleanup remains identical, preserving all existing functionality.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fix lives entirely in fuzz/api.c, touching only the post-fuzz teardown [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode, so no external API or test code is changed.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is a no-op, so clearing registers to NULL is safe.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This pattern is [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[39mN²[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the string-register count, but REG_MASK is small and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstant, so performance impact is negligible in the fuzz loop.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential side-effects and mitigations:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If a malformed operation leaves a pointer in `vars->strings` that was never [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated by xmlFuzzMalloc or other xml API [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, this logic still safely [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mskips duplicate frees but will free it once. That behavior matches the original [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintent.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No change to dropNode or other cleanup; any memory exclusively owned by [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmlNodes still freed in dropNode.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tests and fuzzing harness are untouched; coverage and crash repro remain [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged except the double-free is resolved.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Code context [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexample range[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for patch application:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   <code_range>fuzz/api.[0m[1;92mc:3570[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3595[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Issue Identification[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The double-free arises in the fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`fuzz/api.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during final cleanup[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < REG_MAX; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The harness’s `opDup` handler for `OP_DUP_STRING` aliases an existing string [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer into a new register slot by calling `[0m[1;35msetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mgetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. Since no new [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation occurs, two slots end up owning the same pointer, causing it to be freed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwice at shutdown.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other string operations [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`copyStr`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m correctly allocate fresh buffers, and node[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduplication and integer duplication do not exhibit this aliasing problem.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Insight and Root Cause[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Root cause: aliasing of `vars->strings` entries in `OP_DUP_STRING` rather than[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeep-copying the pointed-to data.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Required preservation: The harness’s register‐tracking mechanisms and its [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior under simulated OOM failures [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia `xmlFuzzInjectFailure` and [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`uncheckedStrdup`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m must remain intact.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Location[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - File to patch: `fuzz/api.c`.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Function to modify: the `[0m[1;35mopDup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint op[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` switch, specifically the `case [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOP_DUP_STRING:` branch.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Proposed Fix[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the aliasing call [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35msetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mgetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with a deep-copy [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mcopyStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mgetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, preserving the increment of the string [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregister index.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Code change outline:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     case OP_DUP_STRING:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mincStrIdx[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m-        [0m[1;35msetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mgetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+        [0m[1;35mcopyStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mgetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Allocate a fresh copy, avoiding aliasing *[0m[35m/[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         break;[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mcopyStr[0m[1;39m([0m[39moffset, str[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` uses `[0m[1;35muncheckedStrdup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` followed by `setStr`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring each register slot holds an independent buffer.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensures each duplicated string gets its own `malloc`’d buffer, matching the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msemantics of `OP_DUP_STRING` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdeep-copy[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates aliasing in register slots, so the final cleanup loop calls [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlFree` on distinct pointers exactly once each.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserves existing harness logic: OOM simulation, register-slot indexing, and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanup behavior remain untouched.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No external libraries or harness entry points are modified. No test code is [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanged.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Slightly increased memory usage per duplicated string [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtwo buffers instead of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtwo references[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: acceptable for fuzzing.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If `uncheckedStrdup` fails under injected OOM, `copyStr` will pass `NULL` to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`setStr`, and the harness frees the old pointer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, then stores `NULL`. This [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmirrors behavior of other copy operations and is safe.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No new memory leaks are introduced: all buffers are still tracked in [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vars->strings` and freed on cleanup.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. Similar Patterns in Codebase[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other string-copy operations [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in `OP_XML_SET_CONTENT`, or when ingesting[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfresh input[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already use `xmlStrndup` and `setStr`.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The helper `copyStr` exists precisely to perform deep copies; leveraging it [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhere aligns with existing style.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Open `fuzz/api.c`.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Locate the `[0m[1;35mopDup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint op[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` function, find the `case OP_DUP_STRING:` branch [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m1022[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Change the body from:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mincStrIdx[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35msetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mgetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      to:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mincStrIdx[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;35mcopyStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mgetStr[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Rebuild and rerun fuzzing under AddressSanitizer to confirm the double-free [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis resolved.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root-Cause Analysis and Location[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The double-free arises in the harness’s final “cleanup” loop in [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/libxml2/fuzz/api.c, around line [0m[1;36m3578[0m[39m.  That loop unconditionally calls [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     for every slot in the fixed-size array, but because the same pointer value can[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreside in multiple slots [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdue to wrap-around in setStr/copyStr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the cleanup frees [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same allocation more than once.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is the only place in the harness that ever frees those string pointers; [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mdropNode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlFreeNode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m does _not_ touch vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy: Deduplicate and Nullify During Cleanup[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Modify the cleanup loop so that each _distinct_ non-NULL pointer in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m is freed exactly once, and every slot is nulled out afterwards to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoid stale pointers.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Pseudocode for the new cleanup:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < REG_MAX; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         xmlChar *p = vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mp == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             continue;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Has this pointer already been freed by an earlier slot?[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         bool dup = false;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; j < i; j++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 dup = true;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 break;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!dup[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Clear this slot to avoid any future access[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = NULL;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[39mN²[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m check is acceptable because REG_MAX is small [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m or [0m[1;36m64[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open `src/libxml2/fuzz/api.c`.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the existing cleanup block around line [0m[1;36m3578[0m[39m:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < REG_MAX; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Replace it with the deduplicating loop:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          int i, j;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < REG_MAX; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              xmlChar *p = vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mp == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  continue;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Skip if already freed in an earlier slot[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; j < i; j++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == p[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                      p = NULL;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                      break;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Null out slot in all cases[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = NULL;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Save and rebuild.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We still free every pointer _once_, preserving the harness’s memory hygiene.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do not alter fuzzer entry points, flags, or external library behavior. [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFuzzing logic and test harness interfaces remain intact.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We only enhance robustness in the final cleanup, eliminating double-free [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout leaking unique allocations.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and Side-Effect Mitigation[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By checking for duplicates in earlier slots, we ensure that pointers stored [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple times are only freed on their first encounter.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Nullifying each slot guarantees that no stale pointer remains after the loop.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Memory usage remains the same; at worst, the last duplicate slots incur only a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpointer comparison and early skip.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is no impact on libxml2 library code or production paths—only the fuzz [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness’s cleanup is tweaked.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Similar Patterns[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This pattern of [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[39mN²[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m deduplication before free is a common idiom in small [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfixed-size registries [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee e.g. the “registry cleanup” in other fuzz harnesses [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder fuzz/[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWith this targeted cleanup change, the double-free is eliminated in all cases, and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe harness continues to free every unique string buffer exactly once. [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1078[0m[39m:   [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1081[0m[39m:    cur->standalone = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1082[0m[39m:    cur->compression = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[39m* not initialized *[0m[35m/[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1083[0m[39m:    cur->doc = cur;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1084[0m[39m:    cur->parseFlags = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1085[0m[39m:    cur->properties = XML_DOC_USERBUILT;[0m                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1094[0m[39m:   [0m[1;35mxmlRegisterNodeDefaultValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmlNodePtr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mcur[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1095[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mreturn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcur[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1096[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
