[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1099[0m[39m: * xmlFreeDoc:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1100[0m[39m: * @cur:  pointer to the document[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Summary of Root Cause  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The double-free occurs not in libxml2’s core parsing or allocation routines, but[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfuzz/api.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  In particular, the harness maintains a circular [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“string register” [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which holds `xmlChar*` pointers returned by [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvarious API calls [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding calls that duplicate comment text via [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`xmlNewComment`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  At teardown of each fuzz iteration, the harness naively walks [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe entire `vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` array and calls `[0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on each non-NULL slot.  If[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same `xmlChar*` value is present in two or more slots, the harness will call [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` on that address multiple times, triggering the observed ASan [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. High-Level Strategy  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   We need to ensure that each distinct heap allocation in `vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed exactly once.  The simplest, most localized fix is to augment the teardown [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloop in `fuzz/api.c` so that after freeing a pointer, any subsequent occurrences of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat exact pointer in the string register are zeroed out [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand thus not freed [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39magain[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  This eliminates duplicate frees with minimal impact on existing logic and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mretains all other harness functionality unchanged.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Locate the post-test cleanup in `fuzz/api.c`, around lines [0m[1;36m3578[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3585[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39minside [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, just before the node cleanup loop[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Replace the single-pass loop:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < REG_MAX; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      with a “dedupe-and-free” pattern:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```c[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < REG_MAX; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          xmlChar *p = vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mp != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Free this pointer once[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Clear this slot[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = NULL;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Prevent any duplicate frees of the same pointer[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint j = i + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m; j < REG_MAX; j++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == p[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                      vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = NULL;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Ensure that after this change:  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - No pointer in `vars->strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` remains non-NULL for addresses that have [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready been freed.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Every distinct pointer is freed exactly once.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - The rest of the harness teardown [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode cleanup, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains untouched.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach directly addresses the symptom—the harness freeing the same [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation twice—by preventing duplicate frees.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It is a minimal change localized to the fuzz harness teardown code, preserving[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall existing operations and their ordering.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No core libxml2 parsing, data-structure, or utility functions are modified; [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall fuzzer-logic remains compatible with existing tests and with OSS-Fuzz’s [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpectations.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change has negligible performance overhead [0m[1;39m([0m[39man [0m[1;35mO[0m[1;39m([0m[39mREG_MAX^[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m scan per test,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand `REG_MAX` is small and bounded[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By zeroing out duplicates, we also leave the register in a clean state for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequent iterations.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side-Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The harness now uses a nested loop for cleanup, but `REG_MAX` is typically on [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe order of a few dozen slots—insignificant compared to parsing workload.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other register slots [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnodes, other strings[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to be managed and [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfreed exactly as before.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No risk of hiding real double-frees in libxml2 core code, since this only [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeduplicates identical `[0m[1;35mxmlFree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls in the harness.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Verification Plan  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild libxml2 with the patched harness.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run `run_fuzzer api -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m` under ASan; verify that the AddressSanitizer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdouble-free no longer triggers.  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run the existing libxml2 unit-test suite to ensure no regressions.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Optionally, introduce a small regression test in the harness that deliberately[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrites the same pointer into two slots and confirms cleanup still only frees once [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mto guard future changes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
